大鳥氏は武家の名門としてつとに知られる。　発祥は平安期以前へ遡り、長く宮中の武者を統括、ないしそれに準ずる立場にあった。所謂釈天御由緒家のうち、現代まで血脈を伝えた唯一の家である。
Ootori-shi is known as a prestigious samurai family. The origin dates back to before the Heian period, and for a long time he was in charge of or equivalent to the musha in Miyanaka. It is the only so-called Shaten Gosei family that has passed down the bloodline to the present day.

武者集団にして近衛軍筆頭としての六衛府が形成されて後はその総領たる六衛大将領を多く輩出し、のみならず一時期は完全に一族内で世襲さえしていた。　家格の点では現在の覇者足利氏も及ばない。
After the formation of the Rokueifu as the leader of the Imperial Guard as a group of musha, many generals of the Rokuei were produced, and at one point they were completely hereditary within the clan. In terms of family character, it is not as good as the current champion Ashikaga-shi.

Why was Ootori-shi able to retain its position and ability for a thousand years in a world where the rise and fall of prosperity is the norm? The reason may be sought after the miraculous unity that has continued to prevent the internal conflicts that tend to occur in the Gonmon.

家を二つに割って争うような致命的決裂を味わわず、大鳥家は歴史を重ねてきたのだった。　しかし、その良き伝統は近年になって遂に断たれている。
The Ootori family has gone through history without experiencing the deadly rupture of splitting a house in two. However, that good tradition has finally been cut off in recent years.

興隆三〇年。後に大戦前夜と呼ばれる時代のこと。　大和は表面上の平穏こそ保っていたが、水面下では大陸の利権を巡って欧州諸国との緊張を日毎に高め、人々は戦争の気配を察して高揚と肌寒さを覚えていた。
The thirty years of prosperity. It was an era later called the eve of the war. Yamato remained calm on the surface, but under the surface, tensions with European countries over continental interests increased day by day, and people felt uplifted and chilly at the sign of war.

時の大鳥当主は極右思想の信奉者であり、欧州側への譲歩を拒み開戦に備えて軍拡を推し進めるべく日夜活動していた。　その影響力は大きく、国は彼の望む方角へ舵を切る。
The owner of Ootori at that time was a follower of the far-right ideology, and was working day and night to refuse concessions to the European side and promote an arms race in preparation for the start of the war. Its influence is great, and the country steers in the direction he wants.

が、彼と意見を異にしていた弟――香奈枝の父――はそんな情勢を憂えた末、決断。　兄に対して下剋上を起こし、権力を奪取する。
However, his younger brother, Kanae's father, who disagreed with him, made a decision after being worried about the situation. Raises Gekokujo against his brother and seizes power.

当主は幽閉され、間もなく世を去った。暗殺の噂が囁かれたのは無論である――真偽は置いて。　彼には幼い嫡男があったが、これはクーデターの際に直臣の手で救出され、何処かへ逃げおおせている。
The lord was imprisoned and soon died. It goes without saying that rumors of assassination were whispered-aside from the truth. He had a young son, who was rescued by Naomi during the coup d'etat and escaped somewhere.

兄を逐って当主の座に着いた弟は大陸経略を融和の路線に切り替えるべく活動し始めるも、内外の厳しい反発に端から苦闘を強いられることになった。　特に内側、大鳥一門の抵抗が激しく……
The younger brother, who took the position of the head of the family after his brother, began to work to switch the continental strategy to a line of harmony, but he was forced to struggle from the beginning due to severe internal and external opposition. Especially inside, the resistance of the Ootori family is intense ...

結果として一族団結の伝統を踏みにじった弟を心情的にどうにも受け入れ難かったのか。前当主の方針に危惧を抱いていた者は少なくなかったにも拘わらず、彼らはこぞって反抗と怠慢の徒と化した。
As a result, was it difficult to accept the younger brother who trampled on the tradition of clan unity? Although many were worried about the policy of the former head of the family, they all turned into rebellious and negligent.

内部の反発を宥めつつ外部の敵に対処せねばならなかった新当主の政治活動は遅滞し、成果を挙げない。　それでも彼は断念しなかったが、勿論運命はとうに彼の背後まで忍び寄り、指差して笑っていたのである。
The political activities of the new head, who had to deal with external enemies while calming internal opposition, were delayed and unsuccessful. Still, he didn't give up, but of course his fate finally sneaked up behind him, pointing and laughing.

So far, we have labeled the role of water in this process as just a catalyst. The main body is a blacksmith and armor, and water is nothing more than a nail that joins them. But what if it wasn't? What if the blacksmith or armor was rather the catalyst and water was one of the main constituents? Based on this idea, I would like to get into the main subject immediately. But then the reader would only see me as an irresponsible listener. Unfortunately, I have no aspirations for politicians or religions. I will try to suppress the feeling of deviation and start by explaining the rationale for this point.

だからどうしたのか、と諸氏は思われるかもしれない。劔冑の製造に水が必要である以上、水の分布と劔冑の生産状況が一致するのには何の不思議もない、と。だがご存知のはずだ。地球上の水はなにも全てが一つの水源を共有しているわけではないということを。　つまり、劔冑の焼き入れに使われる水は大陸東部の地下水庫を経由するものでなくてはならないのである。この水庫からの供給のない地域、つまり南北アメリカ、アフリカ、オーストラリア等においては、劔冑の製造が過去も現在も行われていない（過去については異論もあることを付記する）。

tsurugi * does not breed. That is a fact. But is it okay to assume that the reason is that it is not a living thing? Why don't you forget the possibility? In other words, tsurugi * itself is an organism born by breeding, but it is possible that it is incomplete as a progeny and has no fertility because it is not perfect. Like Leopon, a child of a leopard and a lion. In this case, the breeding that produces tsurugi * is, of course, forging by a blacksmith.

The blacksmith burns ore, strikes it, and builds a territory of armor. Only tremendous high temperatures allow iron to be processed. Fire iron that roasts the air, but blacksmiths wear it one by one. Burn the skin. Bake the meat. Still, the blacksmith who has lived for this moment endures severe pain with a firm will that is as strong as the iron that he struck, completes all the preparations, and sinks himself in the sacred fountain.
